\usetikzlibrary{decorations.markings}
\usetikzlibrary{math}

\begin{tikzpicture}[>=latex,font=\sffamily,semithick,scale=0.5] %1.75

	\tikzstyle{every node}=[font=\tiny] % \large

	\def \fromColor {green}
	\def \toColor {red}	
	
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\dirSectionRingWidth} { 1.5 pt }
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\fileSectionRingWidth} { 2.2 pt }
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\wordSectionRingWidth} { 1.2 pt }

	\pgfmathsetmacro {\dirRad} { 15 }
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\fileRad} { \dirRad -  \dirSectionRingWidth }
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\wordRad} { \fileRad - \fileSectionRingWidth }
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\interactionRad} { \wordRad - \wordSectionRingWidth }

	\def \wordCount { 443 }

	\pgfmathsetmacro {\wordWidth} { 360 / \wordCount }

	\tikzset{test/.style={
		postaction={
			decorate,
			decoration={
				markings,
				mark=between positions 0 and \pgfdecoratedpathlength step 0.5pt with {
					\pgfmathsetmacro {\myval} {multiply(divide(
						\pgfkeysvalueof{/pgf/decoration/mark info/distance from start}, \pgfdecoratedpathlength),100)};
					\pgfsetfillcolor{\fromColor!\myval!\toColor};
					\pgfpathcircle{\pgfpointorigin}{#1};
					\pgfusepath{fill};}
	}}}}

	\tikzmath{
		function drawInteractionLine(\from, \to) {
			if (\from > \to) then {
				\difference = \from - \to;
	  			\between = \to + \difference / 2;
	 		} else {
				\difference = \to - \from;
	 			\between = \from + \difference / 2;
	 		};
			if (\difference > 180) then {
				\difference = 360 - \difference + 180; % [0,180] %XXX: this causes the wrong between...
			};
			\interactionRadMax = \interactionRad * 0.9;
			\diffReciprocalPercentOfSemiCircle = 1 - \difference / 180; % [1,0] %XXX: this fixes the wrong between by making the radius negative! but the radius is not only negative, also the tendecy was inverted... this is a bug
			\interactionControlsRad = \interactionRadMax * \diffReciprocalPercentOfSemiCircle; % [\interactionRad * 0.9, 0]
			{
				%\pgfmathparse{\between}
				%debug
				%\node [] at ({\between} : \interactionControlsRad) { ctrlrad: \interactionControlsRad; between:  \pgfmathresult};
				%\draw [] (0,0) ({\between} : 0.1) -- ({\between} : \interactionRad);
				\path [test=0.25 pt]
					({\from} : \interactionRad) .. 
					controls ({\between} : \interactionControlsRad) ..
					({\to} : \interactionRad);
			};    
		};
	}

	\newcommand{\drawInteraction}[2]{
	
		\pgfmathparse{#1}
		\pgfmathsetmacro{\from}{\pgfmathresult}
		\pgfmathparse{#2}
		\pgfmathsetmacro{\to}{\pgfmathresult}
		
		\tikzmath{drawInteractionLine(\from,\to);}
	}

	\newcommand{ \fileSectorMiddle }[2] {
		(#1+ (#2 - #1) / 2)
	}
	\def \fileSectorRadMiddle { \fileRad - \fileSectionRingWidth / 2 }
	\newcommand{ \fileTextRot }[1] {
		(#1 - 90)
	}

\begin{tikzpicture}[>=latex,font=\sffamily,semithick,scale=0.8,] % 1 nice; 0.8 fits into latex doc(width only)

\tikzstyle{every node}=[font=\tiny] %\ÃÂÃÂ§iny for 1 and 20

\def \width { 20 } %20 nice; 20 fits into latex doc(width only)
\pgfmathsetmacro {\dirHeight} { -1 }
\pgfmathsetmacro {\fileHeight} { 1.9 }
\pgfmathsetmacro {\wordHeight} { 1 }

\def \interactionHeight { 0.0125 }
\def \wordCount { 443 } %663 overall, 443 in the files displayed

\pgfmathsetmacro {\wordWidth } { \width / \wordCount } % 30 / 663 = 0.045248869


\edef \intRowIdx { 0 }
\newcommand{ \incrementRowIdx } {

	\pgfmathparse { \intRowIdx + 1 } \xdef \intRowIdx { \pgfmathresult }

	%also redefine macro
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\intStartY } { \dirHeight - \fileHeight - \wordHeight - \interactionHeight * \intRowIdx }
	\pgfmathsetmacro {\intEndY } { \intStartY - \interactionHeight }
}

\pgfmathsetmacro {\intStartY } { \dirHeight - \fileHeight - \wordHeight - \interactionHeight * \intRowIdx }
\pgfmathsetmacro {\intEndY } { \intStartY - \interactionHeight }

\newcommand{\drawInteraction}[2]{
	
	\pgfmathparse{#1}
    \pgfmathsetmacro{\from}{\pgfmathresult}
	\pgfmathparse{#2}
    \pgfmathsetmacro{\to}{\pgfmathresult}

	\ifdim \from pt < \to pt

		\def \leftColor{green}
		\def \rightColor{red}	

	\else

		\def \leftColor{red}
		\def \rightColor{green}
		
	\fi

	\fill [left color= \leftColor, right color= \rightColor] 
		(\from, \intStartY) rectangle (\to, \intEndY)-- cycle;

	\incrementRowIdx
}

% file coord offset
\pgfmathsetmacro{\boardFs}				{  									  0 * \wordWidth }
\pgfmathsetmacro{\drawingFs}		{ \boardFs				+ 51 * \wordWidth }

\pgfmathsetmacro{\historyFs}			{ \hashFs				+ 17 * \wordWidth }
%\pgfmathsetmacro{\killerFs}				{ \historyFs			+   6 * \wordWidth }

% word coord offset to the middle of the word section
\newcommand{ \wordOffset }[1] {
	(#1 * \wordWidth - \wordWidth / 2)
}

\def \fileYMax {\dirHeight - \fileHeight}
\def \fileYMin {\dirHeight}
% the xcoord of middle of the file section limited by the factors arg1 and arg2
\newcommand{ \fileTextX }[2] {
	( \wordWidth * (#1 + (#2 - #1) / 2) )
}
\pgfmathsetmacro{\fileTextY } { \fileYMin + (\fileYMax - \fileYMin) / 2 }



% dir ------- y 0 to -1
\draw (0,0) rectangle (\width, \dirHeight);
\node [font=\small] at (\width / 2, \dirHeight / 2) {brainless-0.1.2};

\usetikzlibrary{math}

\begin{tikzpicture}[>=latex,font=\sffamily,semithick,scale=0.8,] % 1 nice; 0.8 fits into latex doc(width only)

	\tikzstyle{every node}=[font=\tiny]

	\tikzmath{
		\numberOfUniquWords = 180;
		\wordAngleDiff = 360 / \numberOfUniquWords;
		\maxWordRad = 15;
		\wordRadOffset = 0.2;
		\maxDistRad = 15;
		function getDistRad(\maxSubExecutions) {
			%return \distRadOffset + \maxDistRad * (\maxSubExecutions / 4739 / 100) / 100;
			%return \maxDistRad - \maxSubExecutions / 8.15;
			%return \maxDistRad - pow(3, pow(\maxSubExecutions / 20, 2) / 42;% steiler am ende 15-3^(((x/20)^2)/42)
			%return \maxDistRad - pow(2, pow(\maxSubExecutions / 90, 2) / 90;%15-2^(((x/180)^2)/180)
			return pow(e, (1800 / (\maxSubExecutions + 650))) - 1.4; %e^(1800/(x+650))-1.4
		};
		function getWordRad(\numberOfExecutions) {
			%return \wordRadOffset + \maxWordRad * (\numberOfExecutions / \execOnePercent) / 100;
			return (pow(2, pow(\numberOfExecutions / 31, 2) / 31) - 1 + \wordRadOffset);%2^(((x/31)^2)/31)-(1-0.1)
		};
		function getAngle(\index) {
				return \wordAngleDiff * \index;
		};
	}
	
	\edef \intWordIdx { 0 }
	\newcommand{ \incrementWordIdx } {
		\pgfmathparse { \intWordIdx + 1 } \xdef \intWordIdx { \pgfmathresult }
	}



%	\node [] at ( 0, 0.2 )
%		{m};

 	\node [] at ( {getAngle(\intWordIdx)} :  {getDistRad(\maxSubExecutions)} )
 		{m};
